```python
def casio(command):
    command = [c.strip() for c in command.split(":")]
    print(command)
    max_iter = 100000
    A=B=C=D=E=F=G=H=I=J=K=L=M=N=x=y=0
    com_command = []
    is_syntax = 0
    for c in command:
        for i,s in enumerate(c[0:-2:1]):
            # If `->` appears twice,mean syntax error
            if s == "-" and c[i+1] == ">":
                is_syntax += 1
                if is_syntax == 2:
                    return "Syntax Error."
                com_command.append((c[:i],c[i+2:]))
        is_syntax = 0
    print(com_command)
    return f"A {A}\nB {B}\nC {C}\nD {D}\nE {E}\nF {F}\n"\
        f"G {G}\nH {H}\nI {I}\nJ {J}\nK {K}\nL {L}\nM {M}\nN {N}\n"
```

```python
command = ["1->A:->B","math.sqrt(B-A):C+A->C:A+1->A"]

import math
runtimes = 1
def casio_pro(commands):
    global runtimes
    import os
    # If the file is not exist,create a new one
    if not os.path.exists("CPU.casio"):
        with open("CPU.casio","w") as f:
            f.write("0\n"*8)
    # Split the command string to normal python data type
    command = [c.strip() for c in commands[runtimes-1].split(":")]
    com_command = []
    is_syntax = 0
    for c in command:
        for i,s in enumerate(c[0:-2:1]):
            # If `->` appears twice,mean syntax error
            if s == "-" and c[i+1] == ">":
                is_syntax += 1
                if is_syntax == 2:
                    raise "Syntax Error."
                com_command.append((c[:i],c[i+2:]))
        if is_syntax == 0:
            com_command.append((c,"trash"))
        is_syntax = 0
    max_iter = 100000
    if runtimes == 1:
        max_iter = 1
    for j in range(max_iter):
        for val,var in com_command:
            # Update the data
            with open("CPU.casio","r") as f:
                a = [float(i.strip()) for i in f.readlines()]
                A,B,C,D,E,F,x,y = a
                temp_dict = dict(zip("ABCDEFxy",[A,B,C,D,E,F,x,y]))
                try:
                    temp_dict[var] = eval(val)
                except:
                    raise "Math Error."
                if "trash" in temp_dict:
                    del temp_dict["trash"]
            with open("CPU.casio","w") as f:
                .write("\n".join([str(i) for i in temp_dict.values()]))
    if runtimes == 1:
        runtimes += 1
        casio_pro(commands)
    elif runtimes == 2:
        return 0

casio_pro(command)

```
# 定义awa函数
define awa
d new uwu
d string uwu Hello World! *UwU*
d addkeep newline uwu
d out uwu
d drop uwu
d end
# 结束定义
# 调用awa函数
call awa
# 清除缓存
drop awa
```

﻿[10:26:42]
[a/Jz/a] Light
```python
command = ["1->A:->B","math.sqrt(B-A):C+A->C:A+1->A"]

import math
runtimes = 1
def casio_pro(commands):
    global runtimes
    import os
    # If the file is not exist,create a new one
    if not os.path.exists("CPU.casio"):
        with open("CPU.casio","w") as f:
            f.write("0\n"*8)
    # Split the command string to normal python data type
    command = [c.strip() for c in commands[runtimes-1].split(":")]
    com_command = []
    is_syntax = 0
    for c in command:
        for i,s in enumerate(c[0:-2:1]):
            # If `->` appears twice,mean syntax error
            if s == "-" and c[i+1] == ">":
                is_syntax += 1
                if is_syntax == 2:
                    raise "Syntax Error."
                com_command.append((c[:i],c[i+2:]))
        if is_syntax == 0:
            com_command.append((c,"trash"))
        is_syntax = 0
    max_iter = 100000
    if runtimes == 1:
        max_iter = 1
    for j in range(max_iter):
        for val,var in com_command:
            # Update the data
            with open("CPU.casio","r") as f:
                a = [float(i.strip()) for i in f.readlines()]
                A,B,C,D,E,F,x,y = a
                temp_dict = dict(zip("ABCDEFxy",[A,B,C,D,E,F,x,y]))
                try:
                    temp_dict[var] = eval(val)
                except:
                    raise "Math Error."
                if "trash" in temp_dict:
                    del temp_dict["trash"]
            with open("CPU.casio","w") as f:
                f.write("\n".join([str(i) for i in temp_dict.values()]))
    if runtimes == 1:
        runtimes += 1
        casio_pro(commands)
    elif runtimes == 2:
        return 0

casio_pro(command)

new prompt,input1,input2,result

out prompt
getchar input1
string prompt 请输入第二个字符串:
out prompt
getchar input2
calc.eq input1 input2 result
string prompt 是否相等:
tostr result result
appendvar prompt result
drop result
addkeep newline prompt
out prompt
drop prompt
```

	"There are no channel lists, so a secret channel name can be used for private discussions.",
	"---",
	"Here are some pre-made channels you can join: " + (shouldGetInfo ? (info.public ? ("(" + info.users + " users online, " + info.chans + " channels existing when you enter this page)") : "(Getting online counts...)") : "(Online counts disabled)"),
	...channels,
	"And here's a random one generated just for you: " + ((!shouldGetInfo)||info.public ? ( "?" + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 8)) : ""),
	"---",

[2ZQ3+0] MaggieLikeTheHackchatUwU
hiyoML漏洞
 USBot事件期间，作为XC聊天室主要维护人员Mr_Zhang，抄袭借鉴CC代码，给XC添加了发送hiyoML消息的新功能。一开始只是用来方便用户使用hiyoML发送网易云音乐听歌，然则后来zzChumo、Hack4r、MuRongPIG等略懂XSS（一种网络攻击手段）的用户发现了此功能的BUG，例如插入<iframe>标签，甚至是通过定时跳转或全屏显示某网页内容来达到XSS注入的效果。

 8月10日晚，ee在XC使用hiyoML发送了大量有关Minecraft的音乐，以此来悼念XC与Minecraft时期美好的XC曾经的鱼。

 第二日下午，鉴于ee在USBot事件后依然保留的管理员的身份，Hack4r让ee在XC发送一段插入hiyoTP记录的代码，想借此达到盗号目的。这使XC站长MelonFish与老管理Mr_Zhang、新管理QiuLingYan等人陷入警戒。MelonFish删除了配置文件，撤销了ee管理员，并通知所有人更换密码。本次事件使发送hiyoML功能暂时被Mr_Zhang屏蔽了。

 第三日，MuRongPIG表示，这段盗号代码本来是他想等到放假后（第二天）再试的，但却被ee抢先了一步。后来，Mr_Zhang参考CC代码，写了一个hiyoML开关来降低此类hiyoML漏洞的风险。

 至于本次盗号是否成功……[数据删除]。该事件结束后，据Hack4r所说，他成功盗取了站长MelonFish和管理员MuRongPIG的密码，还把MelonFish的密码发给了HC其他三位用户（4n0n4me、DPG、ee）。XC被迫修改了salt值（一种加密手段），加长到了20位，并表示除了站长MelonFish外，不会有第二个用户知道XC的salt。

 此事件的终止，标志着大乱动时代高潮的不完美结束。
